info:Superior 2-bed Room
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Friends
info:5 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted March 4, 2024
msg:Ticks all the boxes of an elegant  resort hotel.  Enough staff who understand English for communication at any time to not be a pain. Services were excellent.  A special shout out to Ms. Pan for going out of her way to help us with our train ticket problem.  Our room was spacious and luxurious; bed, linen, toiletries were premium quality. Breakfast had everybody covered.  The hotel, next door up from the busier Pullman hotel is in the most scenic area of Wulingyan. There is a night market and an enclave of restaurants nearby yet oddly the area remains calm and very walkable.
     The hotel is about 7 to 10 rmb ( less than $2) from most places in town an 40 rmb from the fast train station.  We did not use anybody's travel services as it was not difficult to get around.  Locals call this hotel "nabally;" neodalle" will get you a blank stare. Show them the hotel's business card and you'll be fine.
     All in all I'd choose to stay here again and would gladly recommend this hotel to family and friends.  It is well worth a 40% premium over Pullman.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçt‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçg
info:Superior Queen Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Couples
info:10 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted April 24, 2024
msg:Come to Zhangjiajie in mid-April to avoid the peak season. The pre-sale three-day stay before the Spring Festival is super cost-effective, a little more than half the price on weekdays, but it's not the peak season like summer vacation. It also includes two breakfasts. The room is spacious and comfortable. It is worthy of being the best hotel in Wulingyuan area. The breakfast is rich and delicious. It is close to the Charming Xiangxi Theater and 1.5 kilometers away from the landmark gate. Since there are not many people in April, online taxis are available at any time. It only costs 6 yuan to the landmark gate. The temperature is suitable, so you can wear short sleeves and a thin jacket. The grass is green and the flowers are blooming. The whole mountain is full of vitality. The weather forecast shows that it will rain every day, but it may actually be sunny. The weather in the mountainous area changes too much. Remember to play at the foot of the mountain when it rains and go to the mountain when it is sunny. Don't join the crowd and go to the Bailong Elevator, which is just an elevator. This is the off-season. I queued for 2 hours. I personally feel that the scenery of Huangshizhai is better than that of Yuanjiajie. The key is why Huangshizhai doesn't queue up. I got on the cableway with eight out of ten points, especially the Imperial Garden of Huangshizhai. The scenery is really invincible. The key point is that there are few people. Yuanjiajie is also beautiful. Mihuntai, Qiankunzhu, and Tianxia No. 1 Bridge are all good, but they are crowded and accompanied by queues. This is still the off-season. You can imagine what the peak season is like. It is recommended to go to the Natural Great Wall. The scenery is different not far away. It is worth it. Tianzi Mountain is still good, especially Yubi Peak and Fairy Flowers. Listen to the revolutionary story of Marshal He Long, and strongly recommend Shentang Bay and Dianjiangtai. Small area tours do not go, and it does not take much time. Remember to tell the driver of the scenic bus, otherwise it will not stop. Although the Golden Whip Creek Road is long, it is not tiring to walk, because it is almost flat, the canyons in the mountains are cool and there are monkeys to accompany you. Remember to take the Golden Whip Creek when it rains and go up the mountain when it is sunny.
